msg:Recently, due to the national epidemic, it was difficult to get out of Wuhan during the Qingming Festival holiday, so I could only pack a package and pretend to be on vacation ^_^
I have stayed at Zall Marriott during the Chinese New Year, and this time I chose Optics Valley Marriott~
The hotel's anti-epidemic measures are very strict. Enter the parking lot to check each person's itinerary code and green code. You need to check the elevator when you go to the lobby. Check and take pictures for the third time when you check in. I don't know if it can be simplified. After that, send a note, stamp or something, go to the front desk to check in and take photos after checking at the lobby.
The hotel has three orientations, Gaoxin Avenue, Optics Valley 6th Road, and a small road. Because I read the comments before, there may be a large card passing by the road at night, so please ask the front desk to help arrange quiet rooms. Room numbers 1-9 are close to On the side of the small road, although it has reached the rear room, the sound of the big trucks passing by on Gaoxin Avenue can still be heard a little at night, but it is still acceptable. The beautiful front desk helped to upgrade the room to a high floor~
The room is quite big and very new, with a double bed of 1.38 and a long sofa, and a big bathtub! There is a connecting room! It can be arranged when the family is out to play more ^_^
There is no coffee machine in the room, there is a bluetooth speaker! Hair dryer is induction! If you add a smart toilet cover, it will be perfect~
Dinner is 168 per person, excluding wine and canned drinks, and you have to add 38... 4 kinds of free drinks, Sprite, Coke, Lemonade and Grapefruit Juice, which are placed in those big jars, with freshly caught seafood , The small abalone is not added much each time, and the time interval for adding it is relatively long. The Jiwei shrimp seems to be dying at the end... There are also razor clams, small scallops, and the live hot pot is delicious~ There are steamed oysters with garlic, Garlic grilled oysters, freshly made grilled steak, very fragrant, and dessert varieties are also ok, but there is no cake, basically mousse, cheese, ice cream four flavors, favorite chocolate flavor ~ other dishes flavor It's alright~
There are many varieties of breakfast, and it only costs 50 yuan. I have eaten the buffet breakfasts of many five-star hotels in the country. This is the most cost-effective. Some hotels do not have this variety and taste as good as more than 100! Beef noodle yyds, there are several kinds of Chinese breakfast: small noodle nest, bean curd, fried dough sticks, peony noodles nest!
The overall environment is very clean! It's a bit confusing that there is no trash can in the bathroom...
Bath products pursue environmental protection and cost with large bottles~ The taste is OK
The service staff are quite enthusiastic and active~ They will take the initiative to say hello when they meet in the aisle. Manager Xie in the lobby (I don‚Äôt know if I remember the wrong surname) can flexibly help guests solve problems~
In short, it is a star-rated hotel that can be punched in again~
